 Does God have the right to acquire property? There has been a discussion since the Supreme Court verdict whether God has the legal right to acquire property and make a case? On this, Jitendra Mohan Sharma, Vice President and Senior Advocate of Supreme Court Bar Association, says that the Gods and Goddesses of Hindus in India are considered as juristic person, and they have all the legal rights like ordinary people
 unhone bataaya ki devi-devataaon ko sampatti arjeet karne, bechney, kharidne, transfar karne or nyaayalay cese ladane samet sabhi kanoonee adhikaar hote hai
 Can the Gods and Goddesses make a case in the court? According to Sharma, Senior Advocate of the Supreme Court, a case can be filed against Hindu Gods and Goddesses like ordinary people
 jab unase sawaal kiya gaya ki devi-devtaa aam insaanon kii tarah soch or vichaar nahin kar saktaa he, to wo kaise sampatti kaa hastantaran karenge, to sinir edwocket jitendra mohan sharma ne kaha ki jis tarah company legal person hoti he or apane diarector yaa trustee ke jariye sampatti arjeet karti he or kaamkaaj karti he, usee tarah hindu devi-devtaa bhi apane pratinidhi ke jariye apane kanoonee adhikaron kaa istemaal karte hai
 He said that the deities of Hindus also acquire property like a company or a minor and fight cases in the court through a representative
 hinduon ke devi-devataaon ko hindu uttaradhikaar adhinium ke tahat sampatti ke adhikaar milte hai
 Civil cases can be made against Hindu deities, but criminal cases cannot be made
 ram lalaa virajman ko supreme court main hui lambii bahessupreme court ke edwocket jitendra mohan sharma ne bataaya ki ayodhya maamle main bhiram lalaa virajmanke cese karne or sampatti arjeet karne samet sabhi kanoonee adhikaar ko lekar lambii bahes hui thi
 Subsequently, the Supreme Court considered Ram Lala Virajman as a legal person
 supreme court baar association ke upaadhyaksh sharma ne yah bhi bataaya ki hinduon ke devi-devataaon yanijuristic persanako natural person yani aam insaanon kii tarah moulik adhikaar nahin die gaye hai
 This means that the natural person is given both the fundamental rights and the legal rights given in the constitution, while the juristic person is given only legal rights

 There is hardly a person among us who does not like green vegetables, but very few people will know that our favorite vegetables are remembered as idioms and proverbs
 aise shabd hamaari jindagi main kuch aise samaa gaye hai ki kai baar hamen pataa bhi nahin chalata or ham unhen istemaal karte rahete hai
 In such a situation, we are presenting for you some such words and idioms that you will become an instant hit in your group circle
 Not know beans- matlab kisi baat ko na jaananaa yaa phir anbhigya hona
 Not worth a hill of beans - means no use

 to vahinccharrot and stickmem stickka taatpary kisi tarah kii sajaa se lagaaya jaataa he

 As thick as pea soup - means excessive haze or something very dense

 In a pickle - It is also a Hindi proverb that the whole matter falls into pickle or sourness
 arthath dikkaton main funs janaa
 Couch Potato - This noun is given to people who spend most of their time in the couch and bed, watching television and playing video games

 But to say like to drop like a hot potato means to give up something or a person

 lekin ab is seat par govind singh ke bete harsh narayan singh kaa kabja he lekin wo bijepi se vidhayak hai

 2013 chunaav ke nattejeyis chunaav main congress kii paramparaagat seat par bijepi ne send lagaai thi

 unka muqabla bispi ke ramlakhan singh se tha, jinhen 47563 vot hasil hue

 is seat par kul 2

 51 lakh votaron ne apane matadhikaar kaa istemaal kiya

 is chunaav main congress teesri paaydaan par rahi or use 22845 vot hasil hue

 unke pita govind narayan singh rajya ke mukhyamantri rah chuke hai
 Harsh Singh was first elected MLA from Rampur Baghelan in 1980 and then won elections on Congress, BJP and Rashtriya Samata Dal tickets
 harsh singh ke dada avadhesh pratap singh vindhyas pradesh ke pehle mukhyamantri the or aazaadee ke ladaai main unki ahm bhoomika rahi

 yahaan 2003 se bijepi kii sarkaar he or isse pehle 10 saal tak congress ne raaj kiya tha
 In the 2013 assembly elections, BJP formed the government by winning 165 seats out of a total of 230 assembly seats
 congress 58 siton tak simat gai thi

 In Shahjahanpur district of Uttar Pradesh, a government roadways bus crushed four people, one of whom died on the spot while leaving the bus station
 prashasnic adhikariyon ne ghayalon ko jila aspataal main bhartee karaayaa he
 Police officer Nagar Sumit Shukla said that on Friday night a bus came out of the roadways bus stop and stopped ahead while crushing the passengers waiting for the bus
 bas ke intjaar main baithe puvaayan ke 30 varshiya manoj kii bas se kuchalane se ghatnasthal par hi maut ho gai jabaki susheel kumaar, sajid evam icecream kaa thela lagane vaale shamashaad gambhir rup se ghayal ho gaye
 The driver driving the bus escaped on the spot after the incident
 tippaniyan According to the police, after the incident at the roadways bus stop, the administration officials admitted all the injured to the district hospital, out of which the doctors declared Manoj dead
 police ne shav tathaa bas ko kabje main le liya he

 police maamle kii jaanch kar rahi he

 )(hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) har vyakti apane ghar ko khubasurat bananaa chahta he or sukh-shanti se rahanaa chahta he
 But due to the increasing population of cities and lack of habitable land, according to Vastushastra, it is difficult to get the desired land
 aise main logon ko shahari vikaas praadhikaranon yaa nijee bilderon dwaara die ja rahe plot yaa flats lenaa unki majaburi hoti he
 But usually these plots or flats are not completely according to Vastu
 aise ploton yaa flaton main kai prakaar ke vaastudosh hote hai jisase jivan main kai tarah kii pareshaaniyaan aati rahati hai
 According to Indian Vastu Shastra, interior decoration of the house is especially helpful to remove or reduce these Vastu defects
 nihsandeh ghar ke interior decoration main deevaaron ke rang or pardon kii mahatvapurn bhoomika he
 Therefore, the color of the walls and curtains of the house should be chosen properly so that positive energy and prosperity can increase
 alag-alag rang ke parde ghar ko na keval khubasurat banaate hai, balki ghar main positive energy banaae rakhane main sahaayak hote hai
 - Since the purpose of each room of the house is different
 bhartiya vaastushastra ghar ke sabhi kamaron kii putai ek hi rang se nahin karwaani chahie
 - Color has scientific significance for mental peace and sweetness in relationships
 bedrum ko gulabi, aasamaani yaa halke hare rang se putai karwaane se sakaaratmak urja main vruddhi hoti he
 - Red and orange are considered auspicious colors for the kitchen
 toilet or bathrum ke liye safed yaa halkaa nila rang anukool hota he
 - To cover the curtain in the house, keep in mind that the curtains should always be of two color layers
 yadi bedrum purv disha main ho to hare rang ke parde achche hote hai
 - Blue curtains for rooms in north direction and white curtains for rooms in west direction is considered appropriate
 yadi cameraa dakshin disha ke kone par ho to laal rang ke parde upyukt maane gaye hai
 - The drawing room is a very important room in the living room
 is kamare kii deevaaron ko halke nile yaa aasamaani, kriim color, pilaa yaa halke hare rang kaa hona uttam mana gaya he
 Cream, white, golden or brown curtains can be used for this room
 - vivy disha main bane drawing room main halkaa haraa, halakaa slate, safed yaa kriim rang kaa prayog kiya janaa chahie
 If the windows and doors of the drawing room are in the north direction, then curtains designed like blue water waves on a green base are perfect
 - bhartiya vaastushastra ke anusaar ghar kii ceiling brahmasthaan kii bhoomika nibhaati he or isse ghar main positive energy aati he
 If you want to paint the ceiling of your house with pink, yellow, blue, etc
 then stop because white is considered the best color of roofs
 tippaniyan - If a house of worship is built in the house, then these walls should be painted in light blue color because it is a symbol of greatness, peace and concentration
 - shayan kaksh main puujagrih nahin hona chahie, lekin shayankaksh main puja-sthaan bananaa majaburi ho to vahaan parde kii vyavastha bahut jaruri he
 For this, white, light yellow, light pink or golden colored curtains are considered auspicious
 - bhartiya vaastushastra ke anusaar in vaastudosha ko dur yaa kam karne ke liye ghar kii aantarik sajja vishesh madadgaar hoti hai
 Undoubtedly the color and curtains of the walls play an important role in the interior decoration of the house
 - isliye ghar kii deevaaron or pardon ke rang kaa sahi chunaav karnaa chahie taaki sakaaratmak urja or samruddhi main vruddhi ho
 Different colored curtains not only make the house beautiful, but also helps in maintaining positive energy in the house
 - chunki ghar ke har kamare kaa uddeshy alag-alag hota he
 Indian Vastu Shastra should not paint all rooms in the house with the same color
 - maansik shanti or rishton main madhurata ke liye rang kaa vaigyanik mahatv he
 Putting the bedrooms in pink, sky or light green color increases the positive energy
 - kichan ke liye laal or naarangi shubh rang mana jaataa he
 White or light blue color is suitable for toilet and bathroom
 - ghar main pardaa lagaana ho yah dhyaan rakhen ki parde hameshaa do rang kii paraton vaali honi chahie
 If the bedroom is in the east direction, green curtains are good
 - uttar disha ke kamare liye nile parde or pashchim disha ke kamare ke liye safed rang ke parde lagaana uchit mana gaya he
 If the room is at the corner of south direction then red colored curtains are considered suitable
 - drawing room yani baithak ghar kaa kaaphi mahatvapurn cameraa hota he
 The walls of this room are considered to be light blue or sky, cream color, yellow or light green
 is kamare liye kriim, safed, sunahare yaa bhure rang kaa pardon prayog kiya ja saktaa he
 - Light green, light gray, white or cream color should be used in the drawing room made in the aerial direction
 yadi drawing room kii khidkiyaan-daravaaje main uttar disha main hon to hare aadhaar par nile rang se bani jal kii laharon jaisi dizin ke parde uttam hote hai
 According to Indian architecture, the sealing of the house plays the role of Brahmasthan and this brings positive energy to the house
 yadi aap apane ghar kii ceiling ko gulabi, pile, nile aadi rangon se putavana chaahate hai to rukiye kyonki chhaton kaa rang safed hi sarvottam mana gaya he
 The comments - yadi ghar main puja ghar banwaaya he to is deevaaron ko halkaa nila rang se rangavaana chahie kyonki yah viratata, shanti or ekaagratha kaa pratik he
 - There should not be a place of worship in the bedroom, but if there is a compulsion to make a place of worship in the bedroom, then the arrangement of curtains is very important
